#### index  1
If 
$H_{1, 3} \neq H_{2, 3}$
 AND 
$B^-_{1, 3} \not\subset H_{1, 2}$
 AND 
$B^-_{1, 3} \not\subset H_{1, 1}$
 AND 
$H_{1, 2} \cap H_{2, 3} \neq  \emptyset$
 AND 
$B^+_{1, 2} \neq B^+_{2, 3}$

$H_{1, 2} \neq H_{2, 1}$

$H_{1, 3} \neq A - B^-_{2, 3}$
 AND 
$B^+_{1, 3} \cap B^+_{2, 3} \neq  \emptyset$
 AND 
$B^+_{2, 2} \neq B^-_{2, 2}$
Then
equiv

$H_{1, 2} = H_{2, 3}$

 AND 
$B^+_{1, 2} \not\subset B^+_{1, 1}$
Then
non-equiv
